// ReportLevelsPerCallList
let
    Source = ReportLanguagesLevels,
    #"PerCallOnly" = Table.SelectRows(Source, each [ReportLevelCode] = 8500),
    #"RemoveColumns" = Table.RemoveColumns(#"PerCallOnly", {"LanguageStringCode", "LanguageCode", "LanguageString","ReportLevelCode", "ReportLevelString"}),

// ReportLanguagesLevelsParameterList

    Source = ReportLanguagesLevels,
    #"RemoveColumns" = Table.RemoveColumns(Source, {"LanguageStringCode", "LanguageCode", "LanguageString", "ReportLevelCode", "ReportLevelString" }),
    #"TableToList" = Table.ToList(#"RemoveColumns", Combiner.CombineTextByDelimiter(",") )

in
    #"TableToList"

// Language
"English (Australia) - Per Call" meta [IsParameterQuery=true, ExpressionIdentifier=ReportLanguagesLevelsParameterList, Type="Any", IsParameterQueryRequired=true]

// CallQueue
let
	//PerCall = List.Contains({"Per Call", "[US]Per Call", "Par appel"}, #"Report Level 2", Comparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase),
  	PerCall = List.Contains(ReportLevelsPerCallList, Language, Comparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase),
	ReportLevelLanguageCode = List.First(ReportParameters[ReportLanguageCode]),

    ReportByRAName = if List.Last(AuthorizedList[Diagnostics]) = "NOTAUTH" then
        Logical.FromText("TRUE")
    else
        Logical.FromText("FALSE"),

    //form the VAAC API query body in JSON format
    //VAACQueryRequestBody = if #"Report Level" = "Per Call" then
    VAACQueryRequestBody = if PerCall then
      "
      {
      ""Filters"":[
          {
            ""DataModelName"":""Date"",
            ""Value"":"""&DateTime.ToText(#"DateFilter", "yyyy-MM-dd")&""",
            ""Operand"":5
          },
          {
            ""DataModelName"":""HasCQ"",
            ""Value"":""True"",
            ""Operand"":0
          }
      ],
      ""Dimensions"":[
          {""DataModelName"":""DocumentId""},
          {""DataModelName"":""ConferenceId""},
          {""DataModelName"":""DialogId""},
          {""DataModelName"":""UserStartTimeUTC""},
          {""DataModelName"":""EndTime""},
          {""DataModelName"":""CallQueueDurationSeconds""},
          {""DataModelName"":""CallQueueId""},
          {""DataModelName"":""CallQueueIdentity""},
          {""DataModelName"":""CallQueueCallResult""},
          {""DataModelName"":""PSTNConnectivityType""},
          {""DataModelName"":""CallQueueTargetType""},
          {""DataModelName"":""CallQueueAgentCount""},
          {""DataModelName"":""CallQueueAgentOptInCount""}
      ],
      ""Measurements"":[
          {""DataModelName"":""PSTNTotalMinutes""},
          {""DataModelName"":""TotalCallCount""}
      ]
      "
      & CommonQueryParametersString &
      "
      }"
    else // Per Day
      "
      {
      ""Filters"":[
          {
            ""DataModelName"":""Date"",
            ""Value"":"""&DateTime.ToText(#"DateFilter", "yyyy-MM-dd")&""",
            ""Operand"":5
          },
          {
            ""DataModelName"":""HasCQ"",
            ""Value"":""True"",
            ""Operand"":0
          }
      ],
      ""Dimensions"":[
          {""DataModelName"":""Date""},
          {""DataModelName"":""CallQueueId""},
          {""DataModelName"":""CallQueueIdentity""},
          {""DataModelName"":""CallQueueCallResult""},
          {""DataModelName"":""PSTNConnectivityType""},
          {""DataModelName"":""CallQueueTargetType""},
          {""DataModelName"":""CallQueueAgentCount""},
          {""DataModelName"":""CallQueueAgentOptInCount""}          
      ],
      ""Measurements"":[
          {""DataModelName"":""AvgCallDuration""},
          {""DataModelName"":""AvgCallQueueDurationSeconds""},
          {""DataModelName"":""PSTNTotalMinutes""},
          {""DataModelName"":""TotalCallCount""}
      ]
      "
      & CommonQueryParametersString &
      "
      }",

    VAACQueryUrlEncoded = Binary.ToText(Binary.Compress(Text.ToBinary(VAACQueryRequestBody), Compression.GZip), BinaryEncoding.Base64),

    //make the VAAC API http request
    HttpResult = Web.Contents(DataSource,
        [
            Headers = [#"content-type" = "application/json;charset=UTF-8"],
            Query = [#"query" = VAACQueryUrlEncoded],
            ManualStatusHandling={403, 500},                
            Timeout = #duration(0,0,ReportExecutionMinutes,0)
        ]),

    HttpResponse = Value.Metadata(HttpResult),
    Headers = Value.Metadata(HttpResult)[Headers],
    RequestOptions = Value.Metadata(HttpResult)[Request.Options],
    RequestOptionsHeaders = Value.Metadata(HttpResult)[Request.Options][Headers],
    RequestOptionsQuery = Value.Metadata(HttpResult)[Request.Options][Query],
    RequestOptionsManualStatusHandling = Value.Metadata(HttpResult)[Request.Options][ManualStatusHandling],
    HttpResponseCode = Value.Metadata(HttpResult)[Response.Status],
    QueryFolding = Value.Metadata(HttpResult)[QueryFolding],

    QID = VAACcontents[requestId],

    QueryRequestID = if HttpResponseCode = 200 then
      VAACcontents[requestId]
    else
      "NOTAUTH",

    UnauthorizedViews = if HttpResponseCode = 200 then
            VAACcontents[unauthorizedViews]
        else
            "",

    UnauthorizedViewsFlag = if UnauthorizedViews = null then
      false
    else
      List.Contains(VAACcontents[unauthorizedViews], "CallQueue"),

    VAACcontents = if HttpResponseCode = 200 then
      Json.Document(HttpResult)
    else
      error 
      [
        Reason = "Server returned an error",
        Message = Text.FromBinary(HttpResult)
      ],

    //convert the VAAC API JSON into a PBI/PowerQuery Table and supply the column names
    //DataResultTable = if HttpResponseCode <> 200 and #"Report Level" = "Per Call" then
    DataResultTable = if (HttpResponseCode <> 200 or UnauthorizedViewsFlag) and PerCall then
         Table.FromRows(
         {
            {"", "", "", Date.ToText(DateTime.Date(Date.AddDays(DateTime.LocalNow(),  0)), "yyyy-MM-dd")&"T00:00:00", Date.ToText(DateTime.Date(Date.AddDays(DateTime.LocalNow(),  0)), "yyyy-MM-dd")&"T00:00:00", 0, "", "NOTAUTHCQ", "NOTAUTHCQ", "0", "", 0, 0, 0, 0}
         },
         {"DocumentID", "ConferenceID", "DialogID", "rawUserStartTimeUTC", "rawEndTime", "rawCallQueueDurationSeconds", "rawCallQueueId", "rawCallQueueIdentity", "rawCallQueueCallResult", "rawPSTNConnectivityType", "rawCallQueueTargetType", "rawCallQueueAgentCount", "rawCallQueueAgentOptInCount", "rawPSTNTotalMinutes", "rawTotalCallCount"})

      //else if HttpResponseCode <> 200 and #"Report Level" = "Per Day" then
      else if (HttpResponseCode <> 200 or UnauthorizedViewsFlag) and not PerCall then
         Table.FromRows(
         {
            {Date.ToText(DateTime.Date(Date.AddDays(DateTime.LocalNow(),  0)), "yyyy-MM-dd")&"T00:00:00", "", "NOTAUTHCQ", "NOTAUTHCQ", "0", "0", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0}
         },
         {"rawDate", "rawCallQueueId", "rawCallQueueIdentity", "rawCallQueueCallResult", "rawPSTNConnectivityType", "rawCallQueueTargetType", "rawCallQueueAgentCount", "rawCallQueueAgentOptInCount", "rawAvgCallDuration", "rawAvgCallQueueDurationSeconds", "rawPSTNTotalMinutes", "rawTotalCallCount"})

      //else if #"Report Level" = "Per Call" then
      else if PerCall then
        Table.FromRows(VAACcontents[dataResult], {
          "DocumentID",
          "ConferenceID",
          "DialogID",
          "rawUserStartTimeUTC",
          "rawEndTime",
          "rawCallQueueDurationSeconds",
          "rawCallQueueId",
          "rawCallQueueIdentity", 
          "rawCallQueueCallResult",
          "rawPSTNConnectivityType",
          "rawCallQueueTargetType",
          "rawCallQueueAgentCount",
          "rawCallQueueAgentOptInCount",
          
          "rawPSTNTotalMinutes",
          "rawTotalCallCount"
          })
      else // Per day
        Table.FromRows(VAACcontents[dataResult], {
          "rawDate",
          "rawCallQueueId",
          "rawCallQueueIdentity",
          "rawCallQueueCallResult",
          "rawPSTNConnectivityType",
          "rawCallQueueTargetType",
          "rawCallQueueAgentCount",
          "rawCallQueueAgentOptInCount",

          "rawAvgCallDuration",
          "rawAvgCallQueueDurationSeconds",
          "rawPSTNTotalMinutes",
          "rawTotalCallCount"
          }),


	// Per Call Specific Transformations
	#"DupRawColumns-PerCall-UserStartTimeUTC" = if PerCall then
		Table.DuplicateColumn(DataResultTable, "rawUserStartTimeUTC", "UserStartTimeUTC")
	else
		DataResultTable,

	#"DupRawColumns-PerCall-EndTime" = if PerCall then
		Table.DuplicateColumn(#"DupRawColumns-PerCall-UserStartTimeUTC", "rawEndTime", "EndTime")
	else
		#"DupRawColumns-PerCall-UserStartTimeUTC",

	#"DupRawColumns-PerCall-CallQueueDurationSeconds" = if PerCall then
		Table.DuplicateColumn(#"DupRawColumns-PerCall-EndTime", "rawCallQueueDurationSeconds", "CallQueueDurationSeconds")
	else
		#"DupRawColumns-PerCall-EndTime",

	// Per Day Specific Transformations
	#"DupRawColumns-PerDay-Date" = if PerCall then
		#"DupRawColumns-PerCall-CallQueueDurationSeconds"
	else
		Table.DuplicateColumn(#"DupRawColumns-PerCall-CallQueueDurationSeconds", "rawDate", "Date"),

	#"DupRawColumns-PerDay-AvgCallDuration" = if PerCall then
		#"DupRawColumns-PerDay-Date"
	else
		Table.DuplicateColumn(#"DupRawColumns-PerDay-Date", "rawAvgCallDuration", "AvgCallDuration"),

	#"DupRawColumns-PerDay-AvgCallQueueDurationSeconds" = if PerCall then
		#"DupRawColumns-PerDay-AvgCallDuration"
	else
		Table.DuplicateColumn(#"DupRawColumns-PerDay-AvgCallDuration", "rawAvgCallQueueDurationSeconds", "AvgCallQueueDurationSeconds"),

	// Common Transformations
	#"DupRawColumns-CallQueueId" = Table.DuplicateColumn(#"DupRawColumns-PerDay-AvgCallQueueDurationSeconds", "rawCallQueueId", "CallQueueId"),
	#"DupRawColumns-CallQueueIdentity" = Table.DuplicateColumn(#"DupRawColumns-CallQueueId", "rawCallQueueIdentity", "CallQueueIdentity"),
	#"DupRawColumns-CallQueueCallResult" = Table.DuplicateColumn(#"DupRawColumns-CallQueueIdentity", "rawCallQueueCallResult", "CallQueueCallResult"),
	#"DupRawColumns-PSTNConnectivityType" = Table.DuplicateColumn(#"DupRawColumns-CallQueueCallResult", "rawPSTNConnectivityType", "PSTNConnectivityType"),
	#"DupRawColumns-CallQueueTargetType" = Table.DuplicateColumn(#"DupRawColumns-PSTNConnectivityType", "rawCallQueueTargetType", "CallQueueTargetType"),
	#"DupRawColumns-CallQueueAgentCount" = Table.DuplicateColumn(#"DupRawColumns-CallQueueTargetType", "rawCallQueueAgentCount", "CallQueueAgentCount"),
	#"DupRawColumns-CallQueueAgentOptInCount" = Table.DuplicateColumn(#"DupRawColumns-CallQueueAgentCount", "rawCallQueueAgentOptInCount", "CallQueueAgentOptInCount"),
	#"DupRawColumns-PSTNTotalMinutes" = Table.DuplicateColumn(#"DupRawColumns-CallQueueAgentOptInCount", "rawPSTNTotalMinutes", "PSTNTotalMinutes"),
	#"DupRawColumns-TotalCallCount" = Table.DuplicateColumn(#"DupRawColumns-PSTNTotalMinutes", "rawTotalCallCount", "TotalCallCount"),

	#"RequestID" = Table.AddColumn(#"DupRawColumns-TotalCallCount", "RequestID", each QueryRequestID),
  	#"NoNulls" = Table.SelectRows(#"RequestID", each [CallQueueIdentity] <> null),

	#"AddReportLevelLanguageCode" = Table.AddColumn(#"NoNulls", "LanguageCode", each ReportLevelLanguageCode),
	  
	#"AddCQTargetType" = Table.AddColumn(#"AddReportLevelLanguageCode", "CQTargetType", each 
		if [CallQueueCallResult] = "callback_call_timed_out" then
		  "Disconnect"
		else if [CallQueueCallResult] = "transferred_to_callback_caller" then
		  "User"
		else
		  [CallQueueTargetType]),

 	//Convert UTC start & end fields appropriately
	#"CallStartUTC" = if PerCall then
		Table.AddColumn(#"AddCQTargetType", "CSTUTC", each DateTimeZone.FromText([UserStartTimeUTC]&" +00:00"))
	else
		#"AddCQTargetType",

	//#"CallEnd UTC" = if #"Report Level" = "Per Call" then
	#"CallEndUTC" = if PerCall then
		Table.AddColumn(#"CallStartUTC", "CETUTC", each DateTimeZone.FromText([EndTime]&" +00:00"))
	else
		#"CallStartUTC",
	  
	//#"ChangeUTCType" = if #"Report Level" = "Per Call" then
	#"ChangeUTCType" = if PerCall then
		Table.TransformColumnTypes(#"CallEndUTC", {{"CSTUTC", type datetimezone}, {"CETUTC", type datetimezone}})
	else
		#"CallEndUTC",
	  
	//#"Call Start Time Local" = if #"Report Level" = "Per Call" then
	#"CallStartTimeLocal" = if PerCall then
		Table.AddColumn(#"ChangeUTCType", "CallStartTimeLocal", each
			if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC-12:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], -12)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC-11:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], -11)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC-10:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], -10)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC-09:30" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], -9, -30)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC-09:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], -9)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC-08:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], -8)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC-07:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], -7)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC-06:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], -6)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC-05:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], -5)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC-04:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], -4)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC-03:30" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], -3, -30)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC-03:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], -3)    
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC-02:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], -2)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC-01:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], -1)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC-00:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], 0)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC+01:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], +1)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC+02:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], +2)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC+03:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], +3)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC+03:30" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], +3, +30)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC+04:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], +4)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC+04:30" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], +4, +30)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC+05:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], +5)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC+05:30" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], +5, +30)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC+05:45" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], +5, +45)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC+06:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], +6)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC+06:30" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], +6, +30)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC+07:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], +7)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC+08:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], +8)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC+08:45" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], +8, +45)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC+09:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], +9)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC+10:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], +10)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC+10:30" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], +10, +30)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC+11:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], +11)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC+12:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], +12)
			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC+12:45" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], +12, +45)

			else if #"UTC Offset" = "UTC+14:00" then DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], +14)    
			else DateTimeZone.SwitchZone([CSTUTC], 0))
			else
//				#"ChangeUTCType",
				Table.AddColumn(#"ChangeUTCType", "CallStartTimeLocal", each DateTimeZone.FromText([Date]&" +00:00")),

			else

	#"ChangeLocalType" = if PerCall then

	#"ChangeDateOnly" = Table.TransformColumnTypes(#"DateOnly",{{"CallStartDateLocal", type date}, {"Date", type datetime}}),

	#"CQCallResultLegendCode" = Table.AddColumn(#"MergedColumns", "CQCallResultLegendCode",  each
		if [CallQueueCallResult ] = "NOTAUTHCQ" then

		else if [CallQueueCallResult] = "disconnected" and [CQTargetType] = "Disconnect" then
			4012	// Abandoned
		else if [CallQueueCallResult] = "agent_joined_conference" or [CallQueueCallResult] = "transferred_to_agent" then
			4001  // Agent Answered
		else if [CallQueueCallResult] = "transferred_to_callback_caller" then
			4001 // Agent Answered
		else if [CallQueueCallResult] = "overflown" then
			4002 // Overflowed
		else if [CallQueueCallResult] = "timed_out" then
			4003 // Timed Out
		else if [CallQueueCallResult] = "callback_call_timed_out" then
			4003 // Timed Out
		else if [CallQueueCallResult] = "no_agent" then

		else if [CallQueueCallResult] = "NOTAUTHCQ" then
			0 // blank
		else

	#"CQTargetTypeLegendCode" = Table.AddColumn(#"CQCallResultLegendCode", "CQTargetTypeLegendCode",  each

			4011 // Agent Answered (Callback)
		else if [CallQueueCallResult] = "disconnected" and [CQTargetType] = "Disconnect" then
			4012 // Abandoned
		else if [CallQueueCallResult] = "overflown" and [CQTargetType] = "ApplicationEndpoint" then
			4012 // Overflowed (Application)
		else if [CallQueueCallResult] = "overflown" and [CQTargetType] = "ConfigurationEndpoint" then
			4012 // Overflowed (Application)
		else if [CallQueueCallResult] = "overflown" and [CQTargetType] = "MailBox" then
			4014 // Overflowed (Voicemail)
		else if [CallQueueCallResult] = "overflown" and [CQTargetType] = "Disconnect" then

		else if [CallQueueCallResult] = "timed_out" and [CQTargetType] = "User" then

		else if [CallQueueCallResult] = "no_agent" and [CQTargetType] = "ConfigurationEndpoint" then
			4030 // No Agents (Application)
		else if [CallQueueCallResult] = "no_agent" and [CQTargetType] = "MailBox" then

		else if [CallQueueCallResult] = "no_agent" and [CQTargetType] = "Disconnect" then

			4033 // "No Agents (External)
		else if [CallQueueCallResult] = "no_agent" and [CQTargetType] = "User" then
			4034 // No Agents (User)
		else if [CallQueueCallResult] = "NOTAUTHCQ" then
			0 // blank
		else
			4005 // Other
    ),      

    // language work - code fields to numbers
	#"CodesToNumbers" = Table.TransformColumnTypes(#"CQTargetTypeLegendCode",{{"CQConnectivityTypeCode", Int64.Type}, {"CQCallResultLegendCode", Int64.Type}, {"CQTargetTypeLegendCode", Int64.Type}}),

    #"Filtered Rows"

// ReportParameters
let
    PerCall = List.Contains(ReportLevelsPerCallList, Language, Comparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase),

    //Source = if #"Report Level" = "Per Call" then
    Source = if PerCall then
            Table.FromRows(
            {
                {8500, #"Language", #"UTC Offset"}
            },
            {"ReportLevelCode", "ReportLevelLanguageString", "UTC Offset"})
        else  // Per Day
            Table.FromRows(

                {8501, #"Language", "UTC-00:00"}
            },
            {"ReportLevelCode", "ReportLevelLanguageString", "UTC Offset"}),


    #"TransformColumns" = Table.TransformColumnTypes(Source, {{"ReportLevelCode", Int64.Type}, {"ReportLevelLanguageString", type text}}),
    #"ReportLevelLanguageTableJoin" = Table.NestedJoin(#"TransformColumns", "ReportLevelLanguageString", ReportLanguagesLevels, "ReportLevel", "LanguageTable", JoinKind.LeftOuter),
    #"ReportLevelTableJoinExpandTableColumn" = Table.ExpandTableColumn(#"ReportLevelLanguageTableJoin","LanguageTable",{"LanguageCode"}),

    #"ReportLevelCodeTableJoin" = Table.NestedJoin(#"ReportLevelTableJoinExpandTableColumn", {"ReportLevelCode", "LanguageCode"}, ReportStrings, {"StringNumber", "LanguageCode"}, "ReportStrings", JoinKind.LeftOuter),
    #"ReportLevelCodeExpandTableColumn" = Table.ExpandTableColumn(#"ReportLevelCodeTableJoin","ReportStrings",{"String"}),
    #"ReportLevelCodeStringRename" = Table.RenameColumns(#"ReportLevelCodeExpandTableColumn",{{"String", "ReportLevelString"}, {"LanguageCode", "ReportLanguageCode"}}),

    #"ReportLevelLanguageStringTableJoin" = Table.NestedJoin(#"ReportLevelCodeStringRename", {"ReportLevelLanguageString"}, ReportLanguagesLevels, {"ReportLevel"}, "ReportLanguage", JoinKind.LeftOuter),
    #"ReportLevelLanguageStringExpandTableColumn" = Table.ExpandTableColumn(#"ReportLevelLanguageStringTableJoin","ReportLanguage",{"LanguageString"}),
    #"ReportLevelLanguageStringDrop" = Table.RemoveColumns(#"ReportLevelLanguageStringExpandTableColumn", {"ReportLevelLanguageString"}),
    #"LanguageStringRename" = Table.RenameColumns(#"ReportLevelLanguageStringDrop", {{"LanguageString", "ReportLanguageString"}}),

    #"ReorderColumns" = Table.ReorderColumns(#"LanguageStringRename", {"ReportLevelCode", "ReportLevelString", "ReportLanguageCode", "ReportLanguageString", "UTC Offset"})


in
    #"ReorderColumns"

// UTC Offset
"UTC+10:00" meta [IsParameterQuery=true, List={"UTC-12:00", "UTC-11:00", "UTC-10:00", "UTC-09:30", "UTC-09:00", "UTC-08:00", "UTC-07:00", "UTC-06:00", "UTC-05:00", "UTC-04:00", "UTC-03:30", "UTC-03:00", "UTC-02:00", "UTC-01:00", "UTC-00:00", "UTC+01:00", "UTC+02:00", "UTC+03:00", "UTC+04:00", "UTC+04:30", "UTC+05:00", "UTC+05:30", "UTC+05:45", "UTC+06:00", "UTC+06:30", "UTC+07:00", "UTC+08:00", "UTC+08:45", "UTC+09:00", "UTC+09:30", "UTC+10:00", "UTC+10:30", "UTC+11:00", "UTC+12:00", "UTC+12:45", "UTC+13:00", "UTC+14:00"}, DefaultValue="UTC-00:00", Type="Text", IsParameterQueryRequired=true]

// AuthorizedList
let
    Source = Web.Contents("https://api.interfaces.records.teams.microsoft.com/Teams.VoiceApps/historical-report-telemetry/getList"),

    HttpResponse = Value.Metadata(Source),

    HttpResponseCode = Value.Metadata(Source)[Response.Status],

    #"ConvertToJson" = if HttpResponseCode = 200 then
        Json.Document(Source)
    else
        Table.FromRows(
            {
                {"", "", "", "", "", "", "", "NOTAUTH"}
            },
            {"TenantId", "UserId", "CorrelationId", "Region", "AutoAttendantDetails", "CallQueueDetails", "AgentDetails", "Diagnostics"}
        ),   

    #"ConvertToTable" = if HttpResponseCode = 200 then
        Table.FromRecords({#"ConvertToJson"})
    else
        #"ConvertToJson",

    #"ChangeType" = if HttpResponseCode = 200 then
        Table.TransformColumnTypes(#"ConvertToTable",{{"TenantId", type text}, {"UserId", type text}, {"CorrelationId", type text}, {"Region", type text}, {"AutoAttendantDetails", type any}, {"CallQueueDetails", type any}, {"AgentDetails", type any}, {"Diagnostics", type any}})
    else
        Table.TransformColumnTypes(#"ConvertToTable",{{"TenantId", type text}, {"UserId", type text}, {"CorrelationId", type text}, {"Region", type text}, {"AutoAttendantDetails", type text}, {"CallQueueDetails", type text}, {"AgentDetails", type text}, {"Diagnostics", type text}})

in
    #"ChangeType"

// DateFilter
let
    Source = Date.AddDays(DateTime.LocalNow(), -45)
in
    Source

// TemplateVersion
let
    Source = "3.2.2"
in
    Source

// ReportRowCountLimit
let
    Source = 150000
in
    Source

// CommonQueryParametersString
let
    Source = ",#(lf)    ""Parameters"":{#(lf)        ""UserAgent"":""Power BI Desktop V" & TemplateVersion & """#(lf)    },#(lf)    ""LimitResultRowsCount"":" & Text.From(ReportRowCountLimit) & "#(lf)"
in
    Source

// DataSource
let
    Source = "https://api.interfaces.records.teams.microsoft.com/Teams.VoiceAnalytics/getanalytics"
in
    Source

// ReportExecutionMinutes
let
    Source = 2
in
    Source

// AuthorizedListCQ
let
    Source = AuthorizedList,
    #"DropColumns" = Table.RemoveColumns(Source, {"TenantId", "UserId", "CorrelationId", "Region", "AutoAttendantDetails", "AgentDetails", "Diagnostics"}),

    #"ExpandCallQueueDetailsList" =  if List.Last(AuthorizedList[Diagnostics]) = "NOTAUTH" then
        Table.AddColumn(#"DropColumns", "CallQueueId", each "")     
    else
        Table.ExpandListColumn(#"DropColumns", "CallQueueDetails"),
    
    #"ExpandCallQueueDetailsRecord" = if List.Last(AuthorizedList[Diagnostics]) = "NOTAUTH" then
       Table.AddColumn(#"ExpandCallQueueDetailsList", "CallQueueName", each "")     
    else
        Table.ExpandRecordColumn(#"ExpandCallQueueDetailsList", "CallQueueDetails", {"CallQueueId", "CallQueueName"}),

    #"ChangeType" = Table.TransformColumnTypes(#"ExpandCallQueueDetailsRecord",{{"CallQueueId", type text}, {"CallQueueName", type text}})
in
    #"ChangeType"
